	WOLOCFACILITYCODE varchar(25) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	WOSUBLOC1 varchar(30) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	WOSUBLOC2 varchar(30) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	WOSUBLOC3 varchar(30) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,

	DESTSITEFACILITYCODE varchar(25) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	SERIAL varchar(50) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	SAPPROCESSED varchar(1) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	CONSTRAINT PK_ISSREC PRIMARY KEY (SERIALNUM,ITEMFACILITYCODE)
);
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX IDX_ITEMFACILITYCODE_ITEMNUM_TRANSDATE ON MP2DW.dbo.ISSREC (  ITEMFACILITYCODE ASC  , ITEMNUM ASC  , ISSUEDATE ASC  )  
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;

	 INCLUDE ( QTY ) 
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX [_dta_index_ISSREC_ITEM_TRANS_CHARG] ON MP2DW.dbo.ISSREC (  ITEMNUM ASC  , TRANSTYPE ASC  , CHARGETO ASC  )  
	 INCLUDE ( ISSUEDATE , QTY ) 
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX idx_IssRec_IssueDate_TransType ON MP2DW.dbo.ISSREC (  ISSUEDATE ASC  , TRANSTYPE ASC  )  
	 INCLUDE ( AVGUNITCOST , COSTCENTER , ITEMFACILITYCODE , ITEMNUM , QTY , REASON , USERID )

	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;

	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX PURREQ_DATEGEN_IDX ON MP2DW.dbo.PURREQ (  ITEMNUM ASC  , ITEMFACILITYCODE ASC  , DATEGENERATED ASC  )  
	 INCLUDE ( QTYRECEIVED , QTYREQUESTED ) 
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX [_dta_index_xPURREQ_ITEM] ON MP2DW.dbo.PURREQ (  ITEMNUM ASC  )  
	 INCLUDE ( DATEGENERATED , FACILITYCODE ) 
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;

	CONTRACTORDOCSVERIFIED varchar(1) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	SUBSTATUS varchar(12) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	SUBSTATFACILITYCODE varchar(25) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	LASTMODIFIEDBY varchar(15) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	LASTMODIFIEDDOMAIN varchar(15) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	LASTMODIFIEDDATE datetime NULL,
	LASTMODIFIEDTIME datetime NULL,
	ORIGSCHEDSTARTDATE datetime NULL,
	ORIGSCHEDFINISHDATE datetime NULL,
	Transaction_Table_Record_Id int NULL,
	GatekeeperPriority float NULL,
	WOSubType varchar(8) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	WODesc varchar(72) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	DatePlanned datetime NULL,
	PlannerUserid varchar(15) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL,
	FeedbackParts int NULL,
	FeedbackEstTime int NULL,
	FeedbackTools int NULL,
	FeedbackPermits int NULL,
	CONSTRAINT xxxPK_WO PRIMARY KEY (WONUM,CLOSEDATE,FACILITYCODE)
);
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX IX2_WO ON MP2DW.dbo.xxxx_dbo.[WO] (  FACILITYCODE ASC  , REQUESTDATE ASC  , PRIORITY ASC  )  
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;
 CREATE NONCLUSTERED INDEX xIX_WO ON MP2DW.dbo.xxxx_dbo.[WO] (  WONUM ASC  , FACILITYCODE ASC  , WOTYPE ASC  )  
	 WITH (  PAD_INDEX = OFF ,FILLFACTOR = 80   ,SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF , IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF , STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF , ONLINE = OFF , ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON , ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON  )
	 ON [PRIMARY ] ;


-- MP2DW.dbo.SqlReportSubdivision definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE MP2DW.dbo.SqlReportSubdivision;

CREATE TABLE MP2DW.dbo.SqlReportSubdivision (
	SubdivisionId int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
	SubdivisionCode varchar(2) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NOT NULL,
	SubdivisionName varchar(50) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NOT NULL,
	DivisionId int NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT PK_SqlReportSubdivision PRIMARY KEY (SubdivisionId),
	CONSTRAINT FK_SqlReportSubdivision_SqlReportDivision FOREIGN KEY (DivisionId) REFERENCES MP2DW.dbo.SqlReportDivision(DivisionId)
);

-- dbo.EntSC_Completed_WorkOrders source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[EntSC_Completed_WorkOrders]
-- 9/9/2008 GAR View used by BP Scorecard application to automate loading of metrics.
AS  SELECT  REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE AS DBNAME,
            'Completed Workorders (#)' AS INPUT,
            COUNT(1) AS METRIC
    FROM    WO (NOLOCK)
    WHERE   REQUESTDATE > GETDATE() - 730
            AND STATUS <> 'X'
    GROUP BY REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE;


-- dbo.EntSC_Emerg_Urgent_WorkOrders source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[EntSC_Emerg_Urgent_WorkOrders]
-- 9/9/2008 GAR View used by BP Scorecard application to automate loading of metrics.
AS  SELECT  REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE AS DBNAME,
            'Total Emergency or Urgent Work Orders (#)' AS INPUT,
            COUNT(1) AS METRIC
    FROM    WO (NOLOCK)
    WHERE   REQUESTDATE > GETDATE() - 730
            AND WOTYPE IN ( 'EMR', 'URGENT' )
    GROUP BY REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE;


-- dbo.EntSC_Planned_WorkOrders source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[EntSC_Planned_WorkOrders]
-- 9/9/2008 GAR View used by BP Scorecard application to automate loading of metrics.
AS  SELECT  REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE AS DBNAME,
            'Planned Workorders (#)' AS INPUT,
            COUNT(1) AS METRIC
    FROM    WO (NOLOCK)
    WHERE   REQUESTDATE > GETDATE() - 730
      AND EXISTS (SELECT 'a'
                  FROM WOE (NOLOCK)
                  WHERE WO.FACILITYCODE = WOE.WOFACILITYCODE
                    AND WO.WONUM        = WOE.WONUM
                    AND ISNULL (WOE.REGHRS,0) + ISNULL(WOE.OTHRS,0) > 0 )
            AND ( wotype IN ( 'PM', 'PRED' )   OR TASKNUM IS NOT NULL OR PLANNED = 'Y' )
    GROUP BY REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE;


-- dbo.EntSC_Total_WorkOrders source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[EntSC_Total_WorkOrders]
-- 9/9/2008 GAR View used by BP Scorecard application to automate loading of metrics.
AS  SELECT  REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE AS DBNAME,
            'Total Workorders (#)' AS INPUT,
            COUNT(1) AS METRIC
    FROM    WO (NOLOCK)
    WHERE   REQUESTDATE > GETDATE() - 730
    GROUP BY REQUESTDATE,
            FACILITYCODE;


-- dbo.EntSC_Work_Order_Hours source

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[EntSC_Work_Order_Hours]
-- 9/9/2008 GAR View used by BP Scorecard application to automate loading of metrics.
AS  SELECT TOP 2 REQUESTDATE,
            A.WOFACILITYCODE AS DBNAME,
            'WO Hours (MP2) (Hours)' AS INPUT,
            ISNULL(( SUM(REGHRS) + SUM(OTHRS) ), 0) AS METRIC
    FROM    WOE A (NOLOCK),
            WO B (NOLOCK)
    WHERE   A.WOFACILITYCODE = B.FACILITYCODE
            AND A.WONUM = B.WONUM
            AND REQUESTDATE > GETDATE() - 730
    GROUP BY REQUESTDATE,
            A.WOFACILITYCODE;


-- dbo.MASTERINVVEND source

ALTER VIEW dbo.MASTERINVVEND
AS
SELECT     i.ITEMNUM, i.FACILITYCODE, i.DESCRIPTION, i.TYPE, i.UOM, i.ACCTCODE, i.OEMMFG, i.TAXABLE, i.NOTES, i.VOLUME, i.DATEADDED, i.CLASS, 
                      i.WEIGHT, i.COSTCENTER, i.CCFACILITYCODE, i.MODEL, i.LASTEDITDATE, i.UD1, i.UD2, i.UD3, i.UD4, i.UD5, i.UD6, i.UD7, i.UD8, i.UD9, i.UD10, 
                      i.UOW, i.SINGLESOURCE, i.COMMCODE, i.TAXUSECODE, i.TAXUSEDESC, i.EXPALLCODE, i.REFERENCE1CODE, i.REF1FACILITYCODE, i.INACTIVE, 
                      i.ALT_ITEMNUM, i.ALT_DESCRIPTION, i.COMMODITY_CAT_CODE, i.COMMODITY_NAME_CODE, i.SERIALIZED, i.OEMITEM, i.CONSIGNMENTITEM, 
                      i.COMMODITY_CAT_TYPE, v.VENDORID, v.VENDFACILITYCODE, v.MANUFACTID, v.PRIMARYVENDOR, v.VENDORITEMNUM, v.BLANKETPONUM, 
                      v.UNITCOST, v.LEADTIME, v.CONTRACTNUM, v.CONTRACTPAGE, v.CONTRACTPARTNUM, v.UNITQTY, v.UOP, v.MINORDERQTY, v.CATALOGNUM, 
                      v.DATELASTPRICED, v.PACKAGE, v.EFFECTIVEDATE, v.FREIGHTOPTION, v.FREIGHTRATE, v.UPDATEPRICE, v.VENDORNAME, v.AUDITUSERID, 
                      v.AUDITDOMAIN, v.AGREEMENTTYPE, v.AGREEMENTID, v.NEXTEFFECTIVECOST, v.NEXTEFFECTIVEDATE, '' AS EMPTYUNITCOST, 
                      '' AS EMPTYPRICEEFFECTIVEDATE
FROM         dbo.INVY AS i INNER JOIN
                      dbo.INVVEND AS v ON i.ITEMNUM = v.ITEMNUM AND i.FACILITYCODE = v.ITEMFACILITYCODE;


-- dbo.ProjectCodes source

-- MP2DW_ProjectCodes.sql
-- Bill Gross (Beacon Technologies) 2018-11-26
-- This view should be installed in MP2DW (Data Warehouse) only.

ALTER VIEW [dbo].[ProjectCodes]
AS
SELECT        [Database], FACILITYCODE, PROJECTNO, ITS_Number, G1, G2, G3, G4
FROM            MP2_CD_LINK.MP2_CD.dbo.ProjectCodes AS ProjectCodes_1
UNION
SELECT        [Database], FACILITYCODE, PROJECTNO, ITS_Number, G1, G2, G3, G4
FROM            MP2_DX_LINK.MP2_DX.dbo.ProjectCodes AS ProjectCodes_2
UNION
SELECT        [Database], FACILITYCODE, PROJECTNO, ITS_Number, G1, G2, G3, G4
FROM            MP2_GY_LINK.MP2_GY.dbo.ProjectCodes AS ProjectCodes_3
UNION
SELECT        [Database], FACILITYCODE, PROJECTNO, ITS_Number, G1, G2, G3, G4
FROM            MP2_PK_LINK.MP2_PK.dbo.ProjectCodes AS ProjectCodes_4
UNION
SELECT        [Database], FACILITYCODE, PROJECTNO, ITS_Number, G1, G2, G3, G4
FROM            MP2_WP_LINK.MP2_WP.dbo.ProjectCodes AS ProjectCodes_5;

-- dbo.vMOE_Available_Status_By_Status source

ALTER VIEW dbo.vMOE_Available_Status_By_Status
AS
SELECT     TOP 100 PERCENT MAS.Module_Id, MAS.Status_Id, MS1.Status_Name, MAS.Available_Status_Id, MS.Status_Name AS Available_Status_Name, 
                      MS.Read_Only
FROM         dbo.MOE_Available_Status AS MAS WITH (nolock) LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.MOE_Status AS MS WITH (nolock) ON MS.Status_Id = MAS.Available_Status_Id AND MS.Module_Id = MAS.Module_Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.MOE_Status AS MS1 WITH (nolock) ON MS1.Status_Id = MAS.Status_Id AND MS1.Module_Id = MAS.Module_Id
ORDER BY MAS.Module_Id, MAS.Status_Id, MAS.Sort_Order;


-- dbo.vMOE_CMMS_Work_Request source

ALTER VIEW dbo.vMOE_CMMS_Work_Request
AS  SELECT  
			/*MP2.NET CHANGE*/
			FACILITYCODE as Facility_Id,
			WONUM AS CMMS_WR_Id,
            TASKDESC AS Title,
            STATUS AS Status_Id,
            PRIORITY AS Priority_Id
    FROM    dbo.WO;
